


Set Reproducibility


seed = 0
random.seed(seed)
torch.manual_seed(seed)
torch.cuda.manual_seed(seed)
np.random.seed(seed)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
os.environ['PYTHONHASHSEED'] = str(seed)
os.environ["CUBLAS_WORKSPACE_CONFIG"]=":4096:8"
torch.backends.cudnn.deterministic = True
torch.backends.cudnn.benchmark = False
torch.use_deterministic_algorithms(True)
3 hop network



Model Architecture


lr=0.001
optimizer = optim.Adam(model_k_5.parameters(), lr=0.001)
criterion = nn.MSELoss()
Final_Model(
  (encoder): MLP(
    (fc1): Linear(in_features=8, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (fc2): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
  )
  (m): MultiHeadsAttModel(
    (v_linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (q_linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (k_linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (out_linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
  )
  (q_net): Q_Net(
    (concat): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (output_layer): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=3, bias=True)
    (softmax_layer): Softmax(dim=1)
  )
)



Model Hyperparameters


n 10
m 10
k 5
neighbors 8
def_ttl 1000
iot_rate 20
epsilon 0.3
capacity 200000
num_steps 2000
iot_generate_time 10
create_packets_till 400
